Method: 1) 样本诱导替代景观：用不同样本定义经验MSSC近似，利用样本间变化作为全局搜索机制；2) 流动 incumbent 策略：在新样本上通过K-means细化传播质心状态，无需回滚；3) 几何级 shaking：变化样本大小以拓宽探索的替代景观尺度，处理聚类不平衡；4) 异步多智能体系统：竞争式探索独立采样景观，转化为集体搜索智能；5) 自动收敛检测：在达到高质量解后自动停止。

Result: 在22个数据集上与11种对比算法进行实验，证明了Big-means++的有效性、效率和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Big-means++通过创新的样本景观遍历和多种机制协同，有效解决了大数据聚类的可扩展性与全局搜索质量之间的权衡问题。

Abstract: Big data clustering remains challenging: the Minimum Sum-of-Squares Clustering (MSSC) problem underlying K-means is NP-hard, and existing methods either reach poor local minima or require prohibitive metaheuristic hybrids. We target arbitrarily tall data: a fixed feature space may contain arbitrarily many, possibly infinitely many, observations, while the algorithm accesses only finite random samples. We propose Big-means++, an algorithm achieving scalability and global-search quality by curating inputs to MSSC optimization on big data. It orchestrates local K-means refinements into a data-native global search for big data clustering. Rather than optimizing the full-data MSSC objective, Big-means++ traverses sample-induced surrogate landscapes. Each sample defines a distinct empirical MSSC approximation with a perturbed local-optimum structure, turning sample-to-sample variation into a global-search mechanism. Unlike Big-means, a flowing-incumbent strategy propagates centroid state across empirical landscapes through K-means refinements on fresh samples without rollback to a best-so-far solution. This increases mobility and favors stable, high-quality configurations across approximations of the full-data structure. A new shaking mechanism varies sample size geometrically, broadening the surrogate landscapes explored across resolution scales, accounting for cluster imbalance, and improving solution quality. A competitive multi-agent system asynchronously explores independent sampled landscapes, transforming diverse stochastic trajectories into collective search intelligence. Automatic convergence detection stops each agent after attaining a high-quality solution but before further search risks degrading it, while providing a universal speed-quality control. Experiments on 22 datasets against 11 competing algorithms demonstrate the effectiveness, efficiency, and robustness of Big-means++.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Data-free knowledge distillation transfers the knowledge encoded in a teacher model to a student model without access to the original training data. Prior work such as Contrastive Abductive Knowledge Extraction (CAKE) achieves this for classifiers by synthesizing samples near the teacher's decision boundary. In this work, we investigate whether this boundary-seeking principle extends to autoencoder distillation through experiments on the MNIST dataset . To enable a direct comparison, we reformulate continuous reconstruction as a dense, per-feature classification task, allowing the decoder to output categorical logits. We show that boundary-seeking objectives are fundamentally ill-posed in bottlenecked generative architectures. CAKE operates on a single, instance-level objective, but a decoder acts as an array of tightly coupled, feature-level classifiers constrained by a shared low-dimensional bottleneck. Independently sampling contrastive targets for these coupled outputs violates the geometry of the learned latent manifold and produces severe gradient conflicts instead of informative boundary samples. Manifold-aware synthesis bypasses these conflicts entirely and establishes an effective baseline for data-free generative distillation.

### [55] [Knowledge-Guided Cross-Modal Fusion for Adult-to-Pediatric ECG Transfer via Label-Conditioned Contrastive Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15928)
*Xinran Liu,Yuwen Li,Hongxiang Gao,Heyang Xu,Jianqing Li,Zongmin Wang,Chengyu Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PEACE是一个知识引导的多模态ECG预训练框架，通过将诊断标签分解为轴级描述（节律、形态、ST-T）并与ECG信号进行细粒度对齐，在成人数据上预训练后有效迁移到儿科ECG场景，在零样本、少样本和全微调设置下均显著提升性能，尤其适用于儿科标签稀缺的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ECG-文本多模态方法通常在全局样本级别对齐波形与文本，混淆了共现诊断的各自证据；同时，模型主要在成人ECG上预训练，由于儿科标签稀缺，跨年龄域迁移效果差。因此需要一种能够利用诊断标签结构化知识、实现细粒度跨模态对齐的方法，以弥合成人与儿科之间的领域差距。

Method: PEACE包含三个核心组件：(1) 将每个诊断沿节律、形态、ST-T三个轴分解描述，并将阳性标签的轴级描述拼接成三个轴令牌和一个融合嵌入；(2) 标签查询网络（LQN）以诊断标签为查询，对ECG令牌和轴令牌进行交叉注意力对齐；(3) 标签集感知双向对比学习（LSBC）在共享诊断的样本间对齐池化ECG特征与融合嵌入；(4) 课程自适应融合（CAF）根据平滑分类损失和训练进度动态调控对齐强度，减少早期优化干扰。知识分支仅用于训练监督，推理时仅使用ECG信号。

Result: 在ZZU-pECG数据集上，PEACE在零样本、50样本和全微调下分别达到59.39%、81.74%和91.56%的宏平均AUC，在有限监督下显著优于基础模型和知识预训练基线；与领域适应初始化相比，零样本大幅提升，50样本AUC与DANN相当。在PTB-XL上微调后，9个统一标签的宏平均AUC达96.90%。消融实验证实，标签条件化的知识对齐（而非全局文本融合）是儿科迁移增益的关键驱动因素。

Conclusion: PEACE通过结构化的诊断知识分解和细粒度的跨模态对齐策略，有效解决了成人-儿科ECG领域的迁移学习问题，在标签稀缺场景下表现突出，证明了标签条件化知识引导对比学习的有效性。

Abstract: Adult and pediatric electrocardiogram (ECG) interpretation relies on age-sensitive criteria, and models pretrained mainly on adult ECGs often transfer poorly to pediatric populations when pediatric labels are scarce. Existing multimodal ECG--text methods typically align waveforms and text at the global sample level, entangling evidence from co-occurring diagnoses and limiting transfer under this gap. We propose Pediatric-Adult ECG Alignment via Cross-modal Enhancement (PEACE), a knowledge-guided framework pretrained on the largely adult MIMIC-IV ECG corpus. PEACE describes each diagnosis along rhythm, morphology, and ST--T axes and, per recording, composes only positive-label descriptors into three axis tokens and a fused embedding. A label query network (LQN) uses diagnostic labels as queries to cross-attend over ECG tokens and axis tokens, while label set aware bidirectional contrastive learning (LSBC) aligns pooled ECG features with the fused embedding when recordings share diagnoses. Curriculum adaptive fusion (CAF) gates alignment strength according to smoothed classification loss and training progress, limiting disruption during early optimization. The knowledge branch is used only for training supervision; inference uses ECG signals alone. On ZZU-pECG, PEACE reaches macro average AUCs of 59.39%, 81.74%, and 91.56% under zero-shot, 50-shot, and full fine-tuning, with the clearest gains over foundation and knowledge-pretraining baselines under limited supervision; versus domain adaptation initializations, zero-shot improves substantially while 50-shot AUC is comparable to DANN. After fine-tuning on PTB-XL, PEACE reaches 96.90% macro average AUC over nine harmonized labels. Ablations confirm that label-conditioned knowledge alignment, rather than global text fusion, is the key driver of pediatric transfer gains.

### [56] [An Exploratory Study of Single Channel Surface Electromyography for Hand Gesture Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15972)
*Daanish Hindustani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探索了使用单通道表面肌电信号(sEMG)结合轻量级机器学习架构进行十种手势分类的可行性。通过提取时域、频域、高阶过零和相对强度特征，结合Pearson相关性过滤和LDA/PCA降维，使用前馈神经网络、KNN和SVM三种分类器，在四组实验中实现了最高90%的准确率，证明了单通道sEMG系统在低功耗手势识别应用中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的手势识别依赖多通道传感器阵列和计算密集型模型，限制了其在低功耗和嵌入式系统中的实际部署。作者试图探索使用单通道sEMG结合轻量级机器学习模型是否能够实现准确的手势识别，以降低成本并提高系统能效。

Method: 从单通道sEMG信号中提取时域、频域、高阶过零和相对强度等多维特征；使用Pearson相关性过滤去除高相关特征以减少冗余；选择性应用LDA和PCA进行降维；系统评估了三种分类器（前馈神经网络、KNN和SVM）在四组实验中的表现。

Result: 结合时域和频域特征、Pearson过滤以及紧凑型神经网络，在有限的时空信息条件下，手势分类准确率最高可达90%。

Conclusion: 单通道sEMG系统具有在低成本、低功耗手势识别应用中实现有效识别的潜力，为嵌入式部署提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Accurate hand gesture recognition using surface electromyography (sEMG) typically relies on multichannel sensor arrays and computationally intensive models. This limits practical deployment in low-power and embedded systems. This study investigates the feasibility of classifying ten hand gestures using a single sEMG channel combined with lightweight machine learning architectures. Raw sEMG signals were transformed into a comprehensive feature-based representation, including time-domain, frequency-domain, higher-order-crossing, and relative-intensity features. Feature redundancy was reduced using Pearson correlation filtering and the removal of highly correlated features, while dimensionality-reduction techniques (LDA and PCA) were applied selectively. Three classifiers, a feed-forward neural network (NN), k-nearest neighbors (KNN), and a support vector machine (SVM), were systematically evaluated across four experiments. Results demonstrate that combining time and frequency features with Pearson filtering and a compact NN can achieve up to 90 percent accuracy, even with limited temporal and spatial information. These findings highlight the potential of single-channel sEMG systems for cost-effective, low-power gesture-recognition applications.

### [57] [DebrisTracer: Reliable Tracking in Hypervelocity Impact Fast Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15986)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在航空航天应用中，超高速冲击产生的碎片质量和速度分布的可靠估计至关重要，但现有工具在处理这些高噪声、高特异性数据集时精度不足，亟需一种准确且可靠的自动跟踪方法。

Method: 基于现成的拓扑跟踪框架（基于临界点提取与匹配），通过融入领域知识和物理假设进行扩展；自动生成准确可靠的碎片跟踪结果，并支持可解释的时空现象可视化分析。

Result: 在物理验证（预测实验射出的质量和弹坑深度分布）上相比领域专家使用的现有工具显著提升了准确性；统计摘要能够可视化识别碎片群体中的不同状态，证实并细化了领域专家的先验预期。

Conclusion: DebrisTracer在多种冲击角度和物理工况下均有效，证明了拓扑追踪框架结合领域知识在超高速碎片跟踪中的实用性，且代码与数据库已开源。

Abstract: This application paper presents DebrisTracer, a framework for the reliable tracking of debris in hypervelocity impact fast imaging. These noisy and highly specific datasets capture the ejection of a large number of debris fragments after the impact of a projectile launched at hypervelocity into a target material. The reliable estimation of debris mass and speed distributions is of major importance in aerospace applications. We document how to extend an off-the-shelf topology tracking framework based on critical point extraction and matching, in order to incorporate domain knowledge and physical assumptions. Our approach automatically produces an accurate and reliable debris tracking, enabling an interpretable visual analysis of this complex space-time phenomenon. Extensive experiments demonstrate the accuracy improvements provided by our approach over established tools used by domain experts in terms of physical validation, specifically via the prediction of the experimental ejected mass and crater depth profiles. We illustrate the utility of our approach across several use cases (with varying impact angles and physics). We show that our statistical summaries enable the visual identification of distinct regimes within the debris population, corroborating and refining prior expectations of domain experts. Our database and our C++ implementation are available at this address: https://github.com/tloloum/DebrisTracer.

### [58] [Presentation, Not Mechanism: A Render Confound in Deprecation-Aware Memory Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16019)
*Zhaoyang Jiang,Zhizhong Fu,Zicheng Li,Yunsoo Kim,Jiacong Mi,Xuanqi Peng,Fei Teng,Honghan Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了证据状态修订（Evidence-State Revision）中的关键混淆变量：当系统同时改变机制和呈现方式时，性能提升几乎全部来自更易读的呈现，而非细粒度机制本身。在控制呈现后，粗粒度失效机制反而优于精细的RevisionLedger，表明记忆评估应固定渲染方式，且弃用感知系统应部署覆盖查询的最粗粒度保留状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有结构化记忆系统（如带类型边、时间更新和冲突状态）的评估往往同时改变机制和提示呈现方式，导致无法区分性能提升究竟来自机制还是呈现。需要解耦二者，量化细粒度证据状态管理的真实收益。

Method: 构建2,907个高一致性问题的基准，涵盖GitHub、多仓库问题历史、Wikipedia和DyKnow风格时间流。对比三种方法：平面检索（flat retrieval）、粗粒度边失效（coarse edge invalidation）、细粒度RevisionLedger。引入渲染匹配控制（相同布局，禁用弃用标记）以分离呈现混淆。

Result: 渲染匹配控制显示：RevisionLedger看似比平面基线提升+0.182，但几乎全部来自呈现改进；细粒度机制残差与零无显著差异（两种评判器下+0.021至+0.025）。控制呈现后，粗粒度失效是唯一对当前状态查询有效的机制，比精细账本高出0.084。

Conclusion: 记忆评估应固定渲染方式；弃用感知系统应部署覆盖查询的最粗粒度保留状态；溯源主要需要保留失效证据，而非更丰富的类型化信息。

Abstract: AI systems increasingly retrieve from records that revise themselves: issue threads, encyclopedic histories, policy logs, and long conversations. The challenge is not only finding relevant evidence, but deciding which claims remain in force, which were superseded, and when to abstain. Structured memories promise to solve this with typed edges, temporal updates, and conflict status, yet evaluations often change mechanism and prompt presentation together. We study this as Evidence-State Revision, comparing flat retrieval, coarse edge invalidation, and fine-grained RevisionLedger on 2,907 high-agreement questions from GitHub, multi-repo issue histories, Wikipedia, and DyKnow-style temporal streams. A render-matched control (same layout, deprecation disabled) reveals the central confound: when a value is changed and later restored, RevisionLedger appears to beat a flat baseline by +0.182, but almost all the gain comes from easier presentation; the fine-grained mechanism residual is indistinguishable from zero (+0.021 to +0.025 across two judge families). After presentation is controlled, coarse invalidation is the only mechanism that pays for current-state queries, beating the fine ledger by 0.084; the same query-sufficiency principle says provenance mainly needs retained invalidated evidence, not richer typing. Memory evaluations should hold render fixed, and deprecation-aware systems should deploy the coarsest retained state that covers their queries.

### [59] [Constrained Hebbian Learning Supports Efficient Representational Allocation under Structural Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16027)
*Patrick Inoue,Florian Röhrbein,Andreas Knoblauch*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究兴奋性竞争性Hebbian规则在生物代谢约束下是否优于BP和DDTP，发现Hebbian学习能在不显著牺牲任务性能的情况下降低表征成本，表明它是一种突触资源分配机制而非通用分类精度优化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统面临突触维护成本高和连接性有限的代谢约束，这些约束倾向于压缩行为相关信息为低冗余编码模式。本文旨在检验兴奋性竞争性Hebbian规则能否在这些约束下支持突触资源分配，并评估其是否比参考学习规则占据更优的成本-性能区间。

Method: 使用基于变分信息瓶颈的互信息度量量化表征成本；采用三个视听基准数据集（AVE、Kinetics-Sounds、VGGSound100）的固定视听嵌入，隔离下游联想可塑性；在匹配稀疏性和架构约束下，将Hebbian学习与Dense Difference Target Propagation (DDTP) 和反向传播 (BP) 进行比较。

Result: 在主要压缩比较中，Hebbian学习达到比稀疏BP和DDTP更低的任务信息成本（CTI），且CTI值与具有非负权重的浅层BP相当。Hebbian学习并非均匀提升分类性能，而是改变了任务相关信息与表征成本之间的权衡，在多个设置中以较低CTI维持了相近的功能性能。

Conclusion: 结果表明存在成本-性能权衡而非统一的精度提升。给定任务相关信息水平下，Hebbian表征保留更少的输入信息同时保持功能性能，尽管在某些数据集上精度略有下降。这支持将Hebbian学习解释为突触资源分配机制，而非最大化视听分类精度的通用策略。

Abstract: Introduction: Biological systems face anatomical and metabolic constraints, including costly synaptic maintenance and limited connectivity. These constraints favor neural codes that compress behaviorally relevant information into low-redundancy patterns. We test whether an excitatory competitive Hebbian rule can support synaptic resource allocation under such constraints and whether the resulting representations occupy a more favorable cost-performance regime than reference learning rules.
  Methods: Representational cost is quantified using mutual-information-based measures derived from the Variational Information Bottleneck. Experiments use fixed audiovisual embeddings from three audiovisual benchmarks (AVE, Kinetics-Sounds, VGGSound100) to isolate downstream associative plasticity. Hebbian learning is compared with Dense Difference Target Propagation (DDTP) and backpropagation (BP) under matched sparsity and architectural constraints.
  Results: Hebbian learning achieves lower task-information cost (CTI) than sparse BP and DDTP in the main compressed comparisons, while reaching CTI values comparable to shallow BP with nonnegative weights. Rather than uniformly improving classification performance, Hebbian learning shifts the trade-off between task-relevant information and representational cost, yielding lower CTI at comparable functional performance in several settings.
  Discussion: The results indicate a cost-performance trade-off rather than uniform accuracy gains. For a given level of task-relevant information, Hebbian representations retain less input information while preserving functional performance, although accuracy is slightly reduced on some datasets. These findings support interpreting Hebbian learning as a mechanism for synaptic resource allocation rather than as a general strategy for maximizing audiovisual classification accuracy.

</details>

Conclusion: 深度强化学习在金融交易中能显著超越被动策略，DDPG和DQL在牛熊切换环境下均表现稳健；但验证集到测试集的泛化差距表明，在特定市场环境下训练的策略难以直接迁移到不同市场条件，需要更鲁棒的领域适应策略。

Abstract: This paper presents our system for Task 3 of the CLEF 2026 FinMMEval Lab, which requires daily long, flat, or short trading decisions for Bitcoin (BTC) and Tesla (TSLA) using news and historical market data. We formulate the problem as a discrete-action Markov Decision Process and compare four deep reinforcement learning algorithms: Policy Gradient (PG), Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), Deep Q-Learning (DQL), and Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG). The agents use technical indicators, cyclical calendar encodings, and daily news sentiment scores produced by LLaMA 3.2 1B. To reduce overfitting and align training with the objective of outperforming buy-and-hold, we introduce an alpha reward based on excess market return and randomize episode start dates. Hyperparameters are optimized with Ray Tune over 180 trials per algorithm-asset pair, with early stopping and model selection based on validation Sharpe ratio. On the CLEF Task 3 test set, DDPG achieves the strongest overall performance. DQL was selected a priori for the live endpoint because it obtained the highest validation Sharpe ratio, with selection performed without access to the test period. For TSLA, DDPG and DQL achieve cumulative returns of 54.96% and 52.62%, respectively, compared with 16.45% for buy-and-hold. For BTC, DDPG achieves a positive return of 1.58% while buy-and-hold declines by -34.27%. The results also reveal a substantial validation-to-test generalization gap, highlighting the difficulty of transferring policies selected in bull-market conditions to a bear-market regime.

### [61] [Revisiting data-driven dynamic security assessment with a tabular foundation model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16031)
*Olayiwola Arowolo,Maosheng Yang,Jochen Cremer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出使用表格基础模型（TFM）通过上下文学习实现数据驱动的预故障动态安全评估，无需为每个预想事故单独训练模型，仅需少量标注样本即可达到约90%的Macro F1分数，并能泛化到未见过的预想事故。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据驱动动态安全评估方法面临两个局限：需要大量标注数据库为每个预想事故单独训练模型，且模型对未见过的预想事故泛化能力差。本文旨在克服这些限制。

Method: 采用表格基础模型（TFM），通过上下文学习评估稳定性，无需重新训练或超参数优化。单个TFM可同时评估多个预想事故。引入电气距离坐标（EDC）作为连续特征以增强对未见预想事故的泛化能力，并分析了EDC何时有效、何时无效。

Result: 在IEEE 68节点系统上，单个TFM仅需每个预想事故120个标注样本即可达到约90%的平均Macro F1分数，比传统方法少两个数量级。对于未见过的预想事故，仅需10个标注样本配合EDC编码即可匹配最佳迁移学习oracle模型。

Conclusion: 该研究为在电力系统运行中开发和部署基础模型铺平了道路，可应用于多种运行任务。

Abstract: Data-driven pre-fault dynamic security assessment (DSA) rapidly evaluates the dynamic risk of credible contingencies on a power system using machine learning. Existing approaches face two limitations. First, they require a large labelled database for training, with a separate model trained, tuned, and maintained for each contingency in a potentially long list of credible contingencies. Second, the trained models generalize poorly to unseen contingencies. This work addresses the limitations by using a tabular foundation model (TFM) that assesses stability through in-context learning, requiring no retraining or hyperparameter optimization. A single TFM can assess many contingencies at once, removing the need for one model per classifier. We also characterize when the use of electrical distance coordinates (EDC) as continuous features enables generalization of TFM to unseen contingencies and when they do not, demonstrating how a few labelled samples can reliably improve generalization. Through comprehensive case studies on the IEEE 68-bus system, we show that a single TFM attains an average Macro F1 score of about 90% with only 120 labelled samples per contingency, roughly two orders of magnitude fewer than conventionally assumed, without any model retraining or hyperparameter tuning. For new/unseen contingencies, we show that using just 10 labelled samples of the new contingency with EDC encoding matches the best achievable transfer learning oracle model, which requires fully labelled data and is not deployable in practice. Overall, this initial study paves the way towards developing and deploying foundation models for power system operations, with possible applications across multiple operational tasks.

### [62] [DELUGE: Towards Continental-Scale Daily Pluvial Flood Damage Prediction via Interpretable Conditioning on Foundation Model Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16050)
*Yuya Kawakami,Daniel Cayan,Dongyu Liu,Kwan-Liu Ma,Tom Corringham*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建多模态深度学习框架DELUGE，以修正后的NFIP索赔数据（2017-2022）为训练目标，融合灾害、暴露度和脆弱性三要素；在水文气象分支中设计Value Modulator和Temporal Modulator两个参数化模块，基于地形描述子和AlphaEarth基础模型嵌入进行条件化，实现可解释的水文响应参数提取。

Abstract: Pluvial (rainfall-driven) flooding accounts for 45% of National Flood Insurance Program (NFIP) claims in the United States and is harder to predict than its riverine and coastal counterparts, with existing approaches limited to coarse resolution, regional domains, or computationally intensive process-based models unsuitable for daily continental-scale use. We present DELUGE, a multimodal deep learning framework for daily pluvial flood damage prediction at ~1 km resolution and national scale, trained on spatially and temporally corrected NFIP claims (2017-2022) and structured around the hazard, exposure, and vulnerability components of disaster risk. Rather than blanket coverage of the Conterminous United States (CONUS), we model the top 100 highest-claim 75 km cells, distributed nationwide and accounting for ~81% of total pluvial flood claims. Our architectural novelty is a pair of parametric modules in the hydrometeorology branch, a Value Modulator and a Temporal Modulator, conditioned on terrain descriptors and AlphaEarth foundation-model embeddings, that expose directly inspectable hydrological response parameters and provide architecture-level interpretability-by-design. Under a spatial block holdout, DELUGE outperforms tuned Random Forest, XGBoost, and LightGBM baselines by 9% to 30% on a dollar-weighted area under the precision-recall curve (PR-AUC), a metric that emphasizes the rare, high-cost claims of greatest operational interest. Beyond DELUGE, we argue this interpretable conditioning scheme is a transferable pattern for integrating foundation-model embeddings into other geospatial prediction tasks.

### [63] [When Model Merging Rivals Joint Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning: A Task-Vector Geometry Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16062)
*S. Aaron McClendon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文在强化学习设置下，首次将模型合并（TIES、RAM+）与联合多任务训练进行公平比较。在AppWorld基准上，合并方法的表现与联合训练无统计差异。原因在于不同难度任务向量近正交（cosine 0.06-0.10），导致支持度和符号位合并退化接近均匀平均。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型合并被宣传为联合多任务训练的替代方案，但在强化学习场景中，这一替代关系从未被系统性地验证过，因为合并方法正是用于联合模型不可用的情况。作者希望填补这一缺失的比较。

Method: 1）在AppWorld基准上，使用LOOP训练难度-1和难度-2的Qwen3-8B专家；2）用TIES和RAM+进行模型合并；3）与在相同数据上联合训练得到的模型进行对比；4）测量专家任务向量的几何特性（余弦相似度、支持度重叠、随机初始化基底和同运行上限）。

Result: 1）在任务目标完成率上，合并方法与联合RL统计上无差异；2）不同难度专家的任务向量近正交（cosine 0.06-0.10），虽支持度重叠约65%；3）存在一个小的共享方向，随训练增强，反映了学习而非低秩参数化噪声；4）由于方向和支持度解耦，支持度和符号位合并方法退化为近乎均匀平均。

Conclusion: 模型合并能够匹配联合多任务训练的效果，但原因并非合并方法的精妙设计，而是在专家向量近正交的几何特性下，不同合并方法实际上等价于简单平均。研究者应警惕合并方法在特定几何结构下看似有效实则退化的现象。

Abstract: Model merging is promoted as a substitute for joint multi-task training, yet in the reinforcement-learning setting this substitution is essentially never tested against the baseline it claims to replace: methods merge independently released agents precisely because a joint model is unavailable. We build the missing comparison. Training difficulty-1 and difficulty-2 Qwen3-8B specialists on the AppWorld agent benchmark with LOOP, we merge them (TIES, RAM+) and pit the result against a jointly trained model on the same data. On task-goal completion, merging matches joint RL -- and every merge variant is statistically indistinguishable. To explain why merge method does not matter here, we measure the geometry of the specialists' task vectors, which carries no task-sampling noise: they are near-orthogonal (cosine 0.06 - 0.10) despite ~65% support overlap, a small, shared direction that grows over training and that we calibrate against a random-init floor and a same-run ceiling to confirm it reflects learning, not the low-rank parameterization. Because direction and support are decoupled, support and sign-based merging (RAM, TIES) collapse to near-uniform averaging. We release all code and statistics.

</details>


### [64] [Physics-Based Deep Spatiotemporal Hyperlocal Radar Nowcasting with a Multi-Variable U-Net for High-Resolution Precipitation Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16080)
*Akshay Sunil,Muhammed Rashid,Raja Sekhar Sivaraju,Sushma Nair,Subimal Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于多仰角雷达反射率、多普勒径向速度和径向速度梯度代理特征的紧凑型U-Net编码器-解码器框架，用于孟买地区90分钟内的降水临近预报。模型通过高反射率注意力模块增强对对流核心的敏感性，并利用物理引导归因确保学习特征的气象可解释性。在2023年5-8月孟买多普勒雷达数据上训练，90分钟预报的CSI分别为0.437(≥10dBZ)、0.332(≥20dBZ)和0.193(≥30dBZ)，优于持续性预报方法，可在标准计算机上秒级运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统高分辨率数值天气预报在短临预报中需要频繁的数据同化、模式初始化和自旋-up，存在计算延迟问题。孟买地区受季风对流、海陆相互作用和局地强降雨影响，短期预测尤为困难。机器学习可直接从高频观测中学习风暴演变，训练后快速生成预报，为解决这一紧迫的实际需求提供了新途径。

Result: 在2023年5-8月孟买多普勒雷达数据上训练，并在时间独立事件上评估。90分钟预报临界成功指数(CSI)：≥10dBZ为0.437，≥20dBZ为0.332，≥30dBZ为0.193。与持续性预报方法相比，模型在较长预报时效下具有更低的RMSE和更高的空间相关性。训练后可在标准计算机上秒级运行生成预报。

Conclusion: 该雷达专用临近预报框架在孟买复杂季风对流环境下实现了高效、准确的短时降水预报，兼具计算速度快(秒级)、物理可解释性(物理引导归因)和对强对流核心敏感(高反射率注意力模块)的优势，为城市洪水管理和实时决策提供了可行的技术方案。

Abstract: Precipitation nowcasting over the immediate 10-90 min period is important for flood management and real-time decision-making in urban regions. Conventional short-range forecasting with high-resolution numerical weather prediction requires frequent data assimilation, model initialization, and spin-up, introducing computational latency. Machine learning provides an alternative by learning storm evolution directly from high-frequency observations and producing forecasts quickly after training. This is particularly relevant for Mumbai, India, where monsoon convection, land-sea interactions, and localized intense rainfall make short-term prediction difficult. Here, we develop a compact radar-only nowcasting framework that combines multi-elevation reflectivity, Doppler radial velocity, and radial-velocity-gradient proxy features within an encoder-decoder U-Net. Using the most recent radar volume scan, the model predicts 12 future composite reflectivity fields at 7.5-min intervals up to 90 min lead time. The derived velocity magnitude, divergence-like, directional-shear, and vorticity-like channels represent kinematic signatures associated with convergence and boundary interactions without requiring full wind-field retrieval. A high-reflectivity attention module improves sensitivity to convective cores, and physics-guided attribution examines whether the learned sensitivities are meteorologically meaningful. The model is trained using Mumbai Doppler radar observations from May to August 2023 and evaluated on temporally independent events. At 90 min lead time, Critical Success Index values are 0.437, 0.332, and 0.193 for $\geq$10, $\geq$20, and $\geq$30 dBZ thresholds, respectively. Compared with persistence, the model gives lower RMSE and higher spatial correlation at longer lead times. ### [65] [Neural spectroscopy of AlphaFold2 reveals encoded protein conformational landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16087)
*Kaustav Mehta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出通过高斯卷积和平滑处理AlphaFold2的权重张量，可以从中提取蛋白质的构象组织信息。该方法（称为神经光谱学）发现，在扰动下，泛素天然接触的断裂顺序与实验一致，KaiB的替代折叠不会恢复，而α-突触核蛋白在不同模型下呈现不同但连贯的构象景观。这些构象信息并非训练目标，而是从结构预测目标中涌现的副产品。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AlphaFold2的9300万参数通常仅被视为序列到结构转换的工具，作者认为这些参数本身可以被直接分析，作为蛋白质构象组织的学习编码，从而揭示模型从训练数据中学到的超越静态结构预测的构象约束。

Method: 对AlphaFold2的Evoformer权重张量进行高斯卷积平滑和缩放处理（称为Scaled Gaussian Convolution），然后通过扰动分析观察构象景观的变化，并使用匹配功率的噪声作为对照实验。

Result: 泛素在扰动下天然接触断裂顺序与几十年折叠实验结果一致；KaiB在五个独立训练模型中均不恢复替代折叠；α-突触核蛋白五个模型产生五种不同但连贯的构象景观；随机噪声产生碎片而非构象。

Conclusion: AlphaFold2的权重编码了超出静态结构预测的构象约束，这些约束从训练数据中涌现为副产品。作者将这种分析方法称为"神经光谱学"，Scaled Gaussian Convolution是其一种具体实现协议。

Abstract: AlphaFold2's 93 million parameters, shaped by the evolutionary record of protein structure encoded in the Protein Data Bank and in sequence alignments, are conventionally treated only as machinery for converting sequence to structure. We propose they are also a scientific object that can be analyzed directly: a learned encoding of protein conformational organization that can be probed and characterized. By smoothing the Evoformer's weight tensors with a Gaussian convolution and scaling the result, we show that the trained model produces physically structured conformational landscapes. Under perturbation, ubiquitin's native contacts break in the order established by decades of folding experiments. For KaiB, five independently trained models agree that the alternative fold is not recovered under perturbation. For alpha-synuclein, five models produce five different but coherent landscapes, mapping where the training signal has determined the representation and where it has not. Matched-power noise controls confirm that random corruption of equal magnitude produces debris, not conformations. The model learned to predict static structures; the conformational organization visible under perturbation was not an explicit training target, suggesting it emerged as a byproduct of that objective. AlphaFold2's weights appear to encode structural constraints, shaped by evolutionary and structural training data, that extend beyond what unperturbed inference reveals. We call the approach of reading them neural spectroscopy, and Scaled Gaussian Convolution one such protocol.

### [66] [DADiff: Diffusion-Driven Cross-Domain Policy Adaptation for Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16090)
*Hanyang Chen,Anirudh Satheesh,Longchao Da,Hua Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出DADiff，一个基于扩散模型的框架，通过生成轨迹偏差估计源域与目标域之间的动力学不匹配，并开发了奖励修改和数据选择两种变体来适应目标域策略，理论证明了策略性能差异受生成轨迹偏差上界约束，实验表明该方法优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习中源域与目标域之间的动力学不匹配（dynamics mismatch）是跨域策略迁移的核心挑战，现有方法依赖域分类器、价值引导数据过滤或表示学习，本文从生成建模视角探索该问题。

Method: 提出DADiff框架，利用扩散模型在下一状态生成过程中捕捉源域与目标域生成轨迹之间的差异来估计动力学不匹配，并开发了奖励修改（reward modification）和数据选择（data selection）两种变体来适应目标域策略。

Result: 在多种偏移设置的环境中进行大量实验，结果表明DADiff在解决动力学不匹配问题上优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 从生成建模角度有效解决了跨域动力学适应问题，理论分析表明策略性能差异受生成轨迹偏差上界约束，且对不同变体的适用性及与先前工作的联系进行了讨论。

Abstract: Transferring policies across domains poses a vital challenge in reinforcement learning, due to the dynamics mismatch between the source and target domains. In this paper, we consider the setting of online dynamics adaptation, where policies are trained in the source domain with sufficient data, while only limited interactions with the target domain are allowed. There are a few existing works that address the dynamics mismatch by employing domain classifiers, value-guided data filtering, or representation learning. Instead, we study the domain adaptation problem from a generative modeling perspective. Specifically, we introduce DADiff, a diffusion-based framework that leverages the discrepancy between source and target domain generative trajectories in the generation process of the next state to estimate the dynamics mismatch. Both reward modification and data selection variants are developed to adapt the policy to the target domain. We also provide a theoretical analysis to show that the performance difference of a given policy between the two domains is bounded by the generative trajectory deviation. More discussions on the applicability of the variants and the connection between our theoretical analysis and the prior work are further provided. We conduct extensive experiments in environments with various shifts to validate the effectiveness of our method. The results demonstrate that our method provides superior performance compared to existing approaches, effectively addressing the dynamics mismatch. We provide the code of our method at https://github.com/hanyang-chen/DADiff-release

### [67] [Understanding Reasoning from Pretraining to Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16097)
*Jingyan Shen,Ang Li,Salman Rahman,Yifan Sun,Micah Goldblum,Matus Telgarsky,Pavel Izmailov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文以国际象棋为受控实验平台，系统研究了预训练（规模、数据）如何影响后续强化学习（RL）后训练阶段的收益，以及RL对模型究竟做了什么。发现：后RL性能可由预训练损失预测，RL奖励曲线的斜率随预训练token数量近似线性增长；RL在简单题上放大SFT已有正确策略，在难题上则挖掘出SFT中几乎不存在的正确走法。该模式在数学领域也得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前RL后训练与预训练被孤立研究，两个基本问题尚未明确：(1) 预训练选择（模型大小、数据）如何影响RL计算收益；(2) RL对模型到底产生了什么影响。标准LLM设置中预训练语料庞大且不受控，难以归因行为来自预训练还是RL，且系统性计算扫描成本过高。

Method: 以国际象棋作为受控测试平台，遵循标准LLM训练流程：在人类对弈数据上预训练5M到1B参数的语言模型，在合成推理轨迹上进行监督微调（SFT），然后在可验证奖励的国际象棋谜题上运行RL。并在数学领域文本上训练1B模型进行迁移验证。

Result: (1) 给定RL计算水平下的后RL性能可由预训练损失很好地预测，RL奖励曲线的斜率随预训练token数量近似线性增长；(2) RL并非简单锐化SFT策略：在简单谜题上放大SFT已偏好的正确走法，在难题上则挖掘出SFT中几乎不存在的正确走法；(3) 该预测模式在数学领域同样成立。

Conclusion: 提供了预训练到RL接口的定量解释，并构建了一个用于研究完整预训练到后训练流水线中推理科学原理的受控测试平台。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become central to improving large language models (LLMs) on complex reasoning tasks, yet RL post-training is largely studied in isolation from the pretraining that precedes it. As a result, two basic questions remain open: (1) how do pretraining choices (model size, data) shape the returns to RL compute, and (2) what does RL actually do to the model? These questions are difficult to study in the standard LLM setting: pretraining corpora are vast and uncontrolled, making it hard to attribute behaviors to pretraining versus RL, and systematic compute sweeps across both stages are prohibitively expensive. To address these challenges, we use chess as a controlled testbed for studying reasoning across the full pretraining-to-post-training pipeline. We follow the standard LLM training pipeline by pretraining language models from 5M to 1B parameters on human chess games, supervised fine-tuning on synthetic reasoning traces, and running RL on chess puzzles with verifiable rewards. Using this framework, we find that the post-RL performance at given RL compute level is well-predicted from the pretraining loss, and slope of the RL reward curves improves approximately linearly with the pretraining tokens. Beyond scaling, we find that RL does not simply sharpen the SFT policy: on easy puzzles it amplifies correct moves the SFT policy already preferred, while on hard puzzles it surfaces correct moves that were nearly absent under SFT. We further test whether our findings transfer beyond chess by training a 1B language model on math-domain text, where the same predictive pattern emerges: longer-pretrained checkpoints reach higher post-RL performance and improve faster under RL. In sum, we provide a quantitative account of the pretraining-to-RL interface and a controlled testbed for studying the science of reasoning across the full pretraining-to-post-training pipeline.

### [68] [The Honest Quorum Problem: Epistemic Byzantine Fault Tolerance for Agentic Infrastructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16109)
*Jun He,Deying Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出"认知拜占庭容错"(EBFT)模型，针对基于AI智能体的分布式系统中的"认知故障"问题——即协议合规但语义错误的验证者可能形成有效证书，导致系统达成错误共识。EBFT在传统拜占庭容错基础上引入两个置信索引参数：eδ（拜占庭集外的一致无效背书）和uε（降低活跃性的不可用支持），并推导了语义有效性、共识一致性、活跃性的法定人数阈值条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统SMR和BFT共识假设协议合规即行为正确，但AI智能体验证者可能出现推理错误（认知故障），导致协议合规的验证者仍会背书语义无效的转换。这种故障模式具有高度相关性（因共享模型权重、训练数据等），传统容错模型无法应对。

Method: 定义EBFT容错模型，在传统拜占庭故障界基础上增加eδ和uε两个置信索引参数，分别刻画语义安全风险（无效背书）和活跃性降级（不可用支持）。推导法定人数阈值条件，提出校准方法论以估计这些预算。

Result: 证明了语义有效性、共识一致性、活跃性的充分必要条件，以及可行阈值选择的条件。表明名义上不同的智能体只有在能可测量地减少无效背书或不可用支持的上尾集中度时，才能提升容错能力。

Conclusion: AI智能体验证者引入了一种新型故障模式（认知故障），传统BFT模型不足以保障语义正确性。EBFT为后确定性分布式系统和智能体基础设施提供了更准确的容错建模框架。

Abstract: State machine replication (SMR) and Byzantine fault-tolerant (BFT) consensus guarantee agreement despite a bounded number of arbitrary, colluding faulty participants. However, these guarantees rely on participants outside this set correctly executing the protocol's transition semantics. Agentic validators expose a weaker boundary: an authenticated, responsive, non-equivocating, and protocol-compliant reasoning participant may still endorse a semantically invalid transition due to reasoning errors.
  We call this failure mode an epistemic fault, and the collective phenomenon the Honest Quorum Problem (where "honest" means protocol-compliant, not semantically correct). Such a quorum can satisfy ordinary checks while forming a certificate for an invalid transition. Thus, agreement alone does not guarantee semantic validity or execution safety. Furthermore, because agentic validators often share model weights, training distributions, prompts, or toolchains, they are highly susceptible to correlated epistemic faults.
  We define Epistemic Byzantine Fault Tolerance (EBFT), a fault-tolerance model for agentic infrastructure and post-deterministic distributed systems. EBFT augments the conventional Byzantine fault bound with two separate, confidence-indexed quantities: $e_δ$ bounds coherent invalid endorsements outside the Byzantine set, and $u_ε$ bounds unusable validator support that degrades liveness. These quantities characterize semantic safety risk and liveness degradation independently. We derive quorum-threshold conditions for semantic validity, consensus agreement, liveness, and feasible threshold selection, and outline a calibration methodology for estimating these budgets. We show that adding nominally distinct agents improves fault tolerance only when it measurably reduces the upper-tail concentration of invalid endorsements or unusable support.

### [69] [When Do Multi-Agent Systems Help? An Information Bottleneck Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16133)
*Wendi Yu,Lianhao Zhou,Xiangjue Dong,Sai Sudarshan Barath,Declan Staunton,Byung-Jun Yoon,Xiaoning Qian,James Caverlee,Shuiwang Ji*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从信息瓶颈角度出发，系统解释了多智能体系统（MAS）相对于单智能体系统（SAS）的优势条件：当中继带宽有限时，MAS通过上下文压缩引入效率与信息损失之间的权衡，MAS的优势取决于上下文减少收益是否超过中继信息损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM驱动的多智能体系统在复杂任务中表现出潜力，但其相对于单智能体系统的优势条件尚不明确，性能在不同设置下表现不一致。本文旨在阐明MAS与SAS之间的本质差异及其优势条件。

Method: 提出信息瓶颈视角：SAS在共享上下文中累积完整推理轨迹，而MAS使用隔离的局部上下文并通过有界中继消息连接。理论分析证明在无限中继带宽下MAS可模拟SAS，而在有界中继下压缩引入效率与信息损失间的权衡，形式化为受参数β控制的信息瓶颈问题。通过18个受控实验（5个基准，3个模型规模）验证理论。

Result: MAS在中继接近充分时持续有效，尤其对弱模型帮助显著；当中继导致信息损失时MAS优势减小或逆转，尤其对强模型而言其已能从冗余上下文中提取有用信息，压缩收益有限。

Conclusion: 多智能体设计本质上是信息瓶颈优化问题，该视角解释了有界智能体间通信何时有益或有害。

Abstract: LLM powered multi-agent systems (MAS) have emerged as a promising paradigm for complex tasks. However, their advantages over single-agent systems (SAS) remain unclear, with performance varying inconsistently across settings. Here, we provide an information bottleneck perspective on elucidating the differences between MAS and SAS. Specifically, our key observation is that a SAS accumulates its full reasoning trace in one shared context, while a MAS uses isolated local contexts connected by bounded relay messages. We show that, under infinite relay bandwidth, any SAS can be simulated by a MAS that transmits the full upstream context. Thus, the nontrivial advantage of MAS arises under bounded relays, where compression introduces a fundamental trade-off: reducing redundant context can improve efficiency, but may also incur loss of task-relevant information. We formalize this trade-off as an information bottleneck controlled by an effective parameter $β$, which captures how the balance shifts with model capability, and shows that MAS gains arise when context reduction outweighs relay information loss. We conduct 18 controlled experiments across five benchmarks and three model scales to validate our theoretical studies. We observe that MAS consistently helps when relays are near-sufficient, especially for weaker models. In contrast, MAS gains shrink or reverse when relays incur information loss, especially for stronger models that can already extract useful information from redundant context and thus gain little from compression. Our study shows that multi-agent design is fundamentally an information-bottleneck optimization problem. This perspective explains when bounded inter-agent communication helps or hurts.

</details>


### [70] [Improving Improved Kernel PLS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16138)
*Ole-Christian Galbo Engstrøm*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对改进核偏最小二乘（IKPLS）算法中的两个关键步骤——X旋转矩阵R和Y载荷矩阵Q的计算——进行加速。通过直接求值策略替代逐项累加来优化R的计算，并首次推导出Q的等价关系，将其计算复杂度从Θ(KM)降至Θ(M)。在CPU和GPU上分别实现了约2倍和6倍的总体加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IKPLS算法1和2是现有最快的PLS校准算法之一，但其X旋转矩阵R和Y载荷矩阵Q的计算仍存在优化空间。特别是Q的计算复杂度为Θ(KM)，在响应变量M较大时成为性能瓶颈。作者希望在不改变算法输出结果的前提下，通过数学推导和计算策略优化来加速这两个关键步骤。

Method: 对于R：用直接求值策略（direct evaluation strategy）替代原有的逐项累加（term-by-term accumulation），在保持相同乘法次数的同时实现更好的并行化。对于Q：首次推导出等价关系，证明每个Y载荷可以从同一迭代中已计算的量推导出来（需乘以显式推导出的常数），从而将计算复杂度从Θ(KM)降至Θ(M)。作者在开源Python包ikpls中实现了这些改进，并分别使用NumPy（CPU）和JAX（GPU）进行基准测试。

Result: 两个改进步骤在数学上与原算法等价，生成完全相同的W、P、Q、R、T矩阵。在单独步骤上实现了高达两个数量级的加速；在完整拟合上，CPU加速约2倍，GPU加速约6倍。

Conclusion: 本文通过计算策略优化和数学等价性推导，有效降低了IKPLS算法中关键步骤的计算复杂度，且不改变输出结果。实验验证了在CPU和GPU上的显著性能提升，为大规模PLS应用提供了更高效的实现方案。

Abstract: Improved Kernel Partial Least Squares (IKPLS) algorithms 1 and 2 are among the fastest PLS calibration algorithms. This article focuses on two shared steps, the computation of the $\mathbf{X}$ rotations, $\mathbf{R}$, and the $\mathbf{Y}$ loadings, $\mathbf{Q}$, and accelerates both. For $\mathbf{R}$, term-by-term accumulation is replaced by a direct evaluation strategy that requires the same number of multiplications but parallelizes better on modern hardware. For $\mathbf{Q}$, I identify - to the best of my knowledge, for the first time - equivalences showing that each $\mathbf{Y}$ loading is obtainable, up to explicitly derived constants, from quantities already computed earlier in the same iteration, and I exploit them in IKPLS to reduce the cost of each loading from $Θ\left(KM\right)$ to $Θ\left(M\right)$ operations whenever $M = 1$ or $2 \leq M < K$, with $K$ predictor variables (number of columns in $\mathbf{X}$) and $M$ response variables (number of columns in $\mathbf{Y}$). Both improvements provably yield exactly the same $\mathbf{W}$, $\mathbf{P}$, $\mathbf{Q}$, $\mathbf{R}$, and $\mathbf{T}$ as the original algorithms. Benchmarks with NumPy (CPU) and JAX (GPU) show speedups of up to two orders of magnitude for the isolated steps and of approximately $2\times$ (CPU) and $6\times$ (GPU) for entire fits. Both improvements are implemented in the free, open-source Python package \texttt{ikpls}.

</details>


### [71] [PRISA: Proactive Infrastructure LiDAR Framework for Intersection Safety Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16156)
*Tam Bang,Hussam Abubakr,Emiliano de la Garza Villarreal,Truc Phuong Nguyen,Austin Harris,Toru Hirano,Mina Sartipi,Yunfei Xu,Hoang H. Nguyen*

TL;DR: PRISA是一个模块化基础设施LiDAR框架，利用隐私保护、低光鲁棒的 roadside传感器进行长期交通观测和实时风险检测，包含感知层和即插即用的风险评估模块，后者能自动从累积感知输出中生成训练数据并训练轨迹预测模型，实现运动预测和双重代理安全评估（TTC和PPET），在R-LiViT数据集和实际路口部署验证了实时可行性。

Motivation: 城市交叉路口是多智能体交互最危险的路段，现有系统难以在隐私保护、低光环境和实时性约束下有效预测并预防冲突，亟需一种能够自动训练、实时运行且隐私友好的边缘端风险监测方案。

Method: 提出PRISA框架，包含感知层（基础设施LiDAR）和风险评估模块。风险评估模块自动从历史感知输出中curate站点特定训练数据，无需人工标注；训练轨迹预测模型后进行连续运动预测；采用TTC评估纵向冲突、PPET评估交叉和弱势道路使用者（VRU）交互冲突。

Result: 在R-LiViT数据集和实际信号交叉口部署验证，PPET评估在2.4秒预测范围内端到端延迟为194 ms，TTC检测和感知满足实时约束，证明了对主动多智能体交叉口安全监测的实用可行性。

Conclusion: PRISA框架在真实路口场景中实现了低延迟、隐私保护的实时风险检测，其自动数据curation和轨迹预测能力为智能交通基础设施中的主动安全监测提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Urban intersections are among the most hazardous locations in road networks, posing significant risks to vehicles and vulnerable road users (VRUs) such as pedestrians and cyclists. The complexity of multi-agent interactions demands continuous, real-time monitoring systems capable of anticipating conflicts before they escalate into crashes. We present PRISA, a modular infrastructure LiDAR framework leveraging privacy-preserving, low-light-robust roadside sensors for long-term traffic observation and real-time risk detection at the edge. The framework comprises two core components: a sensing and perception layer and a plug-and-play risk assessment module. The latter automatically curates site-specific training data from accumulated perception outputs to train a trajectory prediction model without manual annotation. It then deploys the trained model for continuous motion forecasting and dual surrogate safety evaluation, using Time-to-Collision (TTC) for longitudinal conflicts and Predicted Post-Encroachment Time (PPET) for crossing and VRU-involved interactions. PRISA is evaluated on the public R-LiViT dataset and deployed on an NVIDIA Jetson AGX Thor at a live signalized intersection in Chattanooga, Tennessee. PPET-based assessment operates at 194~ms end-to-end latency over a 2.4-second predictive horizon, with TTC-based detection and perception remaining within real-time constraints, demonstrating practical feasibility for proactive multi-agent intersection safety monitoring.

</details>


### [72] [Behaviour-Conditioned Neural Processes for Adaptive Residential Short-Term Load Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16168)
*Ramin Soleimani,Andrea Visentin,Dirk Pesch*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种行为条件化的注意力神经过程（Behaviour-Conditioned Attentive Neural Process）框架，通过将推断出的用户行为结构嵌入概率预测模型，实现面向异质家庭的短期负荷概率预测。该方法在SGSC数据集上相比基线ANP在MAE和CRPS上分别平均降低7.9%和6.9%，尤其在有限上下文场景下优势显著。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出行为条件化注意力神经过程框架：1）离散潜变量从上下文推断行为结构，用于解码器条件化；2）连续潜变量捕获跨异质样本的共享功能不确定性；3）训练阶段利用聚类信息提供弱监督，测试阶段仅依赖上下文推断的类别分布进行条件化。

Result: 在SGSC数据集上，最佳变体相比ANP在MAE上平均降低7.9%，CRPS降低6.9%；相比固定窗口确定性基线，在所有预测步长上RMSE更低且MAE相当；有限上下文场景下提升最大。

Conclusion: 行为条件化的神经过程框架能够以单模型实现跨异质家庭、上下文长度和预测步长的概率负荷预测，支持不确定性量化，验证了将行为结构嵌入预测机制的有效性。

Abstract: Residential short-term load forecasting (STLF) is challenging because household demand is heterogeneous, temporally variable, and shaped by diverse behavioural routines. This work investigates whether inferred behavioural structure can be embedded within the forecasting mechanism of a Neural Process-based probabilistic model, rather than used only as an external grouping signal, for context-conditioned residential STLF. We propose a behaviour-conditioned Attentive Neural Process framework that treats each load profile as a forecasting task. Behavioural structure is represented by a discrete latent variable inferred from the available context and used for behaviour-conditioned decoder conditioning, while a continuous latent variable captures shared functional uncertainty across heterogeneous profiles. To enable conditioning without ground-truth behavioural labels, clustering-derived information provides weak supervision during training, whereas test-time conditioning relies only on context-inferred class distributions. Experiments on the Smart Grid, Smart City (SGSC) dataset use user-disjoint train/validation/test splits, variable context lengths, and multi-step forecast horizons, with comparisons against a label-agnostic ANP baseline and fixed-window deterministic STLF baselines. The proposed variants improve MAE and CRPS over ANP across horizons and context settings, with the largest gains under limited context. The best-performing variant achieves average reductions of 7.9% in MAE and 6.9% in CRPS relative to ANP. Compared with fixed-window baselines, this variant achieves lower RMSE across all evaluated horizons while maintaining competitive MAE, suggesting fewer large prediction deviations under heterogeneous consumption patterns. These results support single-model, uncertainty-aware forecasting across heterogeneous households, contexts, and horizons.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Muon将最终窗口验证成功率从0.290提升至0.546（+88%）；在高学习率下，Muon将GRPO成功率从0.161提升至0.268；在1e-5学习率下，GraphGPO Muon达到0.901成功率，归一化验证AUC从0.399提升至0.556，达到0.5和0.75成功率分别提前30和60次更新。

Abstract: Muon is competitive with AdamW in large-scale pre-training, but its value for reinforcement-learning (RL) post-training remains unclear. We study vanilla Muon in sparse-reward agentic RL through matched single-seed comparisons with AdamW on ALFWorld using Qwen2.5-0.5B-Instruct. Under Group-in-Group Policy Optimization (GiGPO), applying Muon only to hidden weight matrices raises final-window validation success from 0.290 to 0.546 (+88%); high-rate AdamW controls retain no post-update success. The effect depends on the advantage estimator and learning rate. At 3e-5, Muon improves GRPO from 0.161 to 0.268, whereas GraphGPO's late-window gap narrows near saturation. At 1e-5, GraphGPO Muon reaches 0.901, raises normalized validation AUC from 0.399 to 0.556, and reaches 0.5 and 0.75 success 30 and 60 updates earlier, respectively. These exploratory results show that Muon can benefit agentic RL and motivate studying the policy optimizer, advantage estimator, and learning rate jointly. Multi-seed and cross-task validation remain open.

Method: 利用物理硬件中由朗之万动力学描述的随机模拟过程实现能量基热力学计算；通过可调能量势在硬件中生成并采样参数化能量基模型；以概率图模型为框架构建和训练各类机器学习模型；基于理论分析和数值研究评估运行时与能耗；采用热噪声驱动的随机模拟超导电路作为初步实验硬件实现。

Conclusion: 该研究为面向概率机器学习的节能热力学硬件指明了发展路径，展示了热力学计算在降低能耗和延迟方面的潜力。

Abstract: To address the escalating energy and latency demands of machine-learning workloads, we introduce a blueprint for an energy-efficient and fast thermodynamic computing stack that leverages stochastic analog processes in physical hardware. In this work, we focus on energy-based thermodynamic computing where the stochastic process is well described by Langevin dynamics with tunable energy potentials. The implementation of such potentials in physical hardware enables us to generate and sample from basic parameterized energy-based models. We demonstrate how to construct and train popular classes of machine learning models based on these hardware-native energy-based models, using the framework of probabilistic graphical models. We analyze the runtime and energy consumption of different models in this thermodynamic paradigm based on theoretical considerations and numerical studies. As a preliminary experimental realization of such hardware, we present our stochastic analog superconducting circuits driven by thermal noise. Together, these results outline a path toward energy-efficient thermodynamic hardware for probabilistic machine learning.

### [75] [PagedWeight: Efficient MoE LLM Serving with Dynamic Quality-Aware Weight Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16184)
*Yuchen Yang,Yifan Zhao,Anisha Dasgupta,Sasa Misailovic*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出PagedWeight，一种运行时动态量化MoE模型权重的方法，根据当前服务场景动态调整专家权重的精度，以平衡KV缓存大小与模型精度之间的权衡。

Conclusion: PagedWeight有效解决了MoE模型在KV缓存密集型服务中权重与缓存之间的内存竞争问题，通过动态量化策略在精度、内存和吞吐量之间实现了更优的平衡。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) is a popular class of large language models (LLMs), offering high efficiency and accuracy. However, in KV-cache-intensive serving scenarios, MoEs often exhibit a tension between the GPU memory requirements of the model weights and the growing KV cache. We propose PagedWeight, a novel management method for MoE LLM serving that dynamically quantizes MoE model's weights at runtime and balances expert-weight precision with the KV cache sizes. PagedWeight exposes and effectively navigates the complex tradeoff between the model's task accuracy, memory consumption, and throughput/latency. Across several memory-sensitive MoE serving scenarios, PagedWeight improves the quality-memory tradeoff over several existing quantization baselines. PagedWeight achieves FP16-equivalent accuracy with up to 72.0% GPU memory savings and 1.94$\times$ throughput improvement, and improves quality over quantization methods by up to 39.3% at a similar memory budget with at most 4.1% throughput loss.

### [76] [Contour Degree of Amoebas of Complete Intersections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15424)
*Mounir Nisse*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文建立了代数环面中光滑完全交线变形虫轮廓实次数的首个普适上界，通过引入对数余法框架将Lang-Shapiro-Shustin的Pfaffian方法从超曲面推广到任意余维，给出了两种维数条件下的显式轮廓次数估计，并利用Bernstein定理获得稀疏混合体积界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将变形虫轮廓实次数的普适上界从超曲面情形推广到任意余维的完全交线，填补高余维情形下该问题的理论空白。

Method: 引入对数余法丛、对数Grassmann映射和行列式秩条件，在对数余法坐标卡上通过Schur补方程刻画临界轨迹，并用Bernstein定理替代总次数论证获得Newton多面体界。

Result: 在n≥2r和n<2r两种维数条件下给出了显式的普适轮廓次数估计，并得到了比普适界更优的稀疏混合体积界。

Conclusion: 建立了高余维情形下变形虫轮廓的普适上界理论，推广了Lang-Shapiro-Shustin理论，并通过对数余法几何给出了变形虫轮廓的新几何解释。

Abstract: We establish the first universal upper bounds for the real degree of the contour of the amoeba of a smooth complete intersection in the algebraic torus. Our approach extends the Pfaffian method of Lang--Shapiro--Shustin from hypersurfaces to arbitrary codimension by introducing a logarithmic conormal framework based on the logarithmic conormal bundle, the logarithmic Grassmann map, and determinantal rank conditions. We prove that, on suitable logarithmic conormal charts, the critical locus is locally defined by Schur--complement equations arising from the logarithmic conormal matrix. This yields explicit universal contour-degree estimates in both regimes $n\ge 2r$ and $n<2r$. We further replace total-degree arguments by Bernstein's theorem to obtain sparse mixed-volume bounds determined by the Newton polytopes of the transformed equations. These estimates are frequently much sharper than the corresponding universal bounds and provide a higher-codimensional analogue of the Lang--Shapiro--Shustin theory together with a new geometric interpretation of amoeba contours through logarithmic conormal geometry.

### [78] [Order and Pascal depth of Pascal finite automorphisms of the plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15466)
*Elżbieta Adamus,Zbigniew Hajto*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了正特征域K上的仿射平面Pascal有限自同构，证明其阶数由Pascal深度决定：|F|=p^{⌈log_p τ_K(F)⌉}，且结合Dolgachev定理得出阶数谱为{1,p,p²}，Pascal深度有上界p²。通过Jung–van der Kulk融合积和Serre树定理给出了GA₂(K)的纯群论证明。构造了达到阶数p²的Witt向量和达到深度p²的显式 tame自同构G_p。与高维情形对比，发现阶数和深度均无界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究正特征域上仿射平面自同构的有限阶性质，特别是Pascal有限自同构的阶数谱和深度上界，并探讨其与高维情形的差异。

Method: 结合Dolgachev关于平面Cremona群的定理，利用Jung–van der Kulk融合积和Serre树定理进行纯群论证明，通过构造Witt向量和显式自同构G_p证明下界紧致性。

Result: Pascal有限平面自同构的阶数谱为{1,p,p²}，Pascal深度τ_K(F)≤p²，且构造了达到阶数p²和深度p²的显式例子；高维情形中阶数和深度均无界。

Conclusion: 平面情形因Cremona群和融合积结构导致阶数和深度有严格上界，而高维情形则无此限制，揭示了正特征域上自同构群维数依赖的深刻差异。

Abstract: Let $K$ be a field of characteristic $p>0$. For a Pascal finite automorphism $F$ of the affine plane we show that its order is determined by its Pascal depth, $|F|=p^{\lceil\log_pτ_K(F)\rceil}$, and that, combined with Dolgachev's theorem on the plane Cremona group, this pins the order spectrum of Pascal finite plane automorphisms to $\{1,p,p^2\}$ and bounds the Pascal depth by $τ_K(F)\le p^2$. For the polynomial group $\text{GA}_2(K)$ we give a second, independent proof of the order-$p^2$ ceiling, a purely group-theoretic argument from the Jung--van der Kulk amalgam and Serre's tree theorem, using no birational geometry. We prove that the bound is sharp in two independent senses. Order~$p^2$ is attained by the length-two Witt vectors, and Pascal depth $p^2$ is attained by an explicit tame automorphism $G_p$, for which we give a characteristic-free proof that $τ_K(G_p)=p^2$. We contrast the plane with higher dimensions, where both order and depth are unbounded.

Method: 将 ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$ 等同于刚性化带框架的 Hurwitz 空间，利用 twisted admissible cover 紧化并添加额外刚性化数据，构造出适当的环面紧化及其 Berkovich 骨架。

Abstract: Let ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$ be the ramification stratum in the parameter space of degree $D \geq 2$ complex polynomials consisting of polynomials with ramification profile $\vecμ^*$.   A non-trivial point is that the tropicalization of ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$ is not available a priori, as the stratum does not come with a previously known proper toroidal compactification. We resolve this issue by identifying ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$ with a rigidified framed Hurwitz space. Using the twisted admissible cover compactification, together with additional rigidifying data, we construct a proper toroidal compactification and hence an associated Berkovich skeleton. We prove that $\mathcal{T}_D(\vecμ^*)$ is isomorphic to this skeleton.
  We further show that the projectivized tree space $\mathbb P\mathcal{T}_D(\vecμ^*)$ compactifies ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$. Finally, we compare this compactification with the DeMarco--McMullen compactification of polynomial moduli by projectivized space of polynomial trees.

### [81] [Curves with a large automorphism group admitting a cyclic subgroup of index $2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15983)
*Arianna Dionigi,Massimo Giulietti,Marco Timpanella*

TL;DR: 本文研究定义在任意特征域上的代数曲线中，包含指数2循环子群的子群（如二面体群、广义拟二面体群等）的阶的上界。主要结果：在特征p≠2的代数闭域上，二面体自同构群的阶满足|H|≤4g(X)+4；并分类了所有非二面体但阶大于4g(X)+4且包含指数2循环子群的群。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用代数几何与群论方法，将曲线定义域从复数域推广到特征p≠2的代数闭域，分析包含指数2循环子群的群结构，给出上界证明和分类结果。

Abstract: The Hurwitz bound on the order of the $\mathbb K$-automorphism group ${\rm{Aut}}({\mathcal{X}})$ of an algebraic curve ${\mathcal{X}}$ of genus $g(\mathcal{X})\ge 2$ defined over a field $\mathbb K$ of zero characteristic states that $|{\rm{Aut}}({\mathcal{X}})|\le 84(g(\mathcal{X})-1)$.   For instance, if a subgroup $H$ of ${\rm{Aut}}({\mathcal{X}})$ is dihedral, then in the complex case, $|H| \leq 4g(\mathcal{X}) + 4$. More recently it has been shown that a tighter bound holds for $H$ a generalized quasi-dihedral group.
  In this paper we explore the more general setting of a curve defined over a field of any characteristic, and $H$ a group admitting a cyclic subgroup of index two. We show that the same upper bound for the size of a dihedral group of automorphisms holds for curves defined over an algebraically closed field of characteristic $p\ne 2$. Then we provide some classification results about (non-dihedral) groups of size larger than $4g(\mathcal{X})+4$ admitting a cyclic subgroup of index $2$.

Abstract: We study rationality of conic bundles over finite fields defined over the line. Using work of Colliot-Thélène and Yang together with Chebotarev density, we compute the asymptotic proportion of such conic bundles that are rational as $q$ goes to infinity.

### [84] [Degenerations of multisingularities and Artin algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16022)
*Jakub Koncki,Richárd Rimányi*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究交换、结合、有限维复Artin代数的退化层次结构，提出基于奇点理论的稳定层次，并证明该层次可由对称性数据（自同构群）通过Thom多项式完全刻画，且推广了传统形变理论中的代数退化层次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的退化研究依赖于Hilbert概形，而本文希望引入一种基于奇点理论的退化概念（稳定层次），从而建立更自然的偏序结构，并探索能否仅从对称性数据（自同构群）确定退化层次。

Method: 利用稳定映射芽的奇点与局部代数之间的对应关系，定义奇点理论意义上的退化（稳定层次）。核心工具是Kazarian建立的多奇点Thom多项式（等变示性类），通过将这些多项式进行合适的替换来完全刻画退化层次。

Result: 1) 在广泛维度范围内，稳定层次可由代数的自同构群（对称性数据）完全确定，计算退化的偏序集成为算法化的。2) 该奇点理论层次扩展了传统形变理论中的代数退化层次——后者要求维数（秩）固定，而新框架允许比较不同维数的代数。

Conclusion: 建立了奇点理论视角下的代数退化层次（稳定层次），证明了其与对称性数据的深刻联系，并推广了经典形变理论的结果，为有限维Artin代数的分类提供了新的工具。

Abstract: We study the degeneration hierarchy of commutative, associative, finite-dimensional complex Artin algebras. Instead of studying degenerations in the Hilbert scheme, we introduce a singularity-theoretic notion of degeneration based on the correspondence between singularities of stable map germs and local algebras. This leads to a natural partially ordered set, the stable hierarchy, in which one algebra degenerates to another if nearby singularities realize the latter.
  Our first main result is that, in a wide range of dimensions, this hierarchy can be determined purely from symmetry data, namely from the automorphism groups of the algebras or singularities. The key tool is the theory of certain equivariant characteristic classes called Thom polynomials of multisingularities, established by Kazarian. Suitable substitutions into these polynomials completely characterize the hierarchy. As a consequence, the computation of degeneration posets becomes algorithmic in nature.
  In our second main result, we prove that our singularity-theoretic hierarchy extends the algebraic hierarchy obtained from deformation theory. While deformation theory requires the dimension (rank) to be fixed, our hierarchy generalizes this framework by comparing algebras of varying dimensions.

</details>

### [85] [Loss of positive definiteness is a symptom, not the cause, of high-Weissenberg-number breakdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15334)
*Yuan Yu,Lanjin Lian,Feiyang Chu*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了高魏森堡数下构象张量失去对称正定性（SPD）对数值计算的影响。经典理论认为SPD丧失导致计算崩溃，但本文证明：在有溶剂粘度分数β>0时，初始值问题对任意对称应力都是局部适定的。作者推导了不定态的理论，发现冻结系数分析给出波数均匀有界的增长率，方向分辨不稳定阈值为λ_min(A) < -β/(1-β)；应力扩散提供闭式截断，而经典σ∝k灾难在溶剂粘度消失时恢复。行列式恒等式表明违规会在λ/2时间尺度上自愈，持续违规反映了重现它的截断误差。谱法和格子玻尔兹曼测试验证了阈值、溶剂分数反转和分辨率独立性。在四辊轧机干预中，强制SPD将爆发延迟15个对流时间，但减少了30%的驻点魏森堡数。五种耦合方案中，局部二阶矩应力源在Wi=50时通过全程预算，同时携带det A≈-8.5×10^5；散度耦合变体在t^*=47失败。幸存方案在Wi=10和20时与已发布基准的偏差分别为0.05%和0.18%。结论：失去正定性既非计算崩溃的必要条件也非充分条件；离散耦合方式起决定性作用，违规是分辨率指标，作者为此提供了运行时监测器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高魏森堡数下数值崩溃常被归因于构象张量失去对称正定性（SPD），但该结论源自无溶剂粘度的麦克斯韦型模型。当存在溶剂分数β>0时，现有理论缺失，研究者希望建立一套定量理论来解释不定态行为及其对数值计算的影响，并澄清SPD丧失与数值崩溃之间的因果关系。

Method: 采用冻结系数分析推导增长率与不稳定阈值；利用行列式恒等式证明违规自愈机制；通过谱法和格子玻尔兹曼方法进行数值验证；在四辊轧机流动中测试强制SPD的效果；比较五种不同耦合方案（包括局部二阶矩应力源和散度耦合变体）的稳定性。

Result: 推导出方向分辨不稳定阈值λ_min(A) < -β/(1-β)；发现违规在λ/2时间尺度上自愈；强制SPD延迟爆发但降低驻点魏森堡数；局部二阶矩应力源在Wi=50时保持稳定（det A≈-8.5×10^5），而散度耦合变体在t^*=47失败；幸存方案与基准偏差极小（Wi=10时0.05%，Wi=20时0.18%）。

Conclusion: 失去对称正定性既非数值计算崩溃的充分条件也非必要条件；离散耦合方式的选择才是决定性因素；违规程度可作为分辨率指标，作者提供了运行时监测器用于实际计算。

Abstract: Numerical breakdown at high Weissenberg number is often attributed to loss of symmetric positive definiteness (SPD) of the conformation tensor. That conclusion follows from Maxwell-type models without solvent viscosity. With solvent fraction $β>0$, the initial-value problem is locally well posed for arbitrary symmetric stress. We derive the missing quantitative theory for indefinite states and test its computational consequences. Frozen-coefficient analysis gives a growth rate uniformly bounded in wavenumber and the direction-resolved instability threshold $λ_{\min}(A)<-β/(1-β)$; stress diffusion supplies a closed-form cutoff, while the classical $σ\propto k$ catastrophe is recovered as solvent viscosity vanishes. A determinant identity shows that violations self-heal on the timescale $λ/2$, so persistent violations measure the truncation error that recreates them. Spectral and lattice Boltzmann tests reproduce the threshold, solvent-fraction reversal, and resolution independence. In four-roll-mill interventions, enforcing SPD delays blow-up by 15 convective times but reduces the stagnation-point Weissenberg number by 30%. Across five coupling schemes, a local second-moment stress source remains stable through the full budget at $\mathrm{Wi}=50$ while carrying $\det A\approx-8.5\times10^5$; the divergence-coupled variant fails at $t^*=47$. The surviving scheme matches published benchmarks within 0.05% and 0.18% at $\mathrm{Wi}=10$ and 20. Thus loss of positive definiteness is neither necessary nor sufficient for breakdown: the discrete coupling route decides, and the violation is a resolution gauge for which we provide run-time monitors.

</details>


### [86] [Atomic Design Transformer: Scaffold-Conditioned 3D Molecule Generation via xTB-Reward Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15918)
*Takao Kotani*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种SE(3)等变的原子设计Transformer（ADT），通过自回归方式逐原子生成3D分子结构。ADT利用局部坐标系编码新原子位置实现SE(3)不变性，主干为纯因果Transformer。引入xTB拓扑保持率（XTP）评估生成质量。预训练模型在GEOM-Drugs数据集上XTP约54%，经强化学习（RLVR）微调后XTP提升至约98%，有效分子产率约95%。此外还提出逆运动学Transformer解决大分子离散误差累积问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D分子生成方法通常需要先确定原子类型和连接方式再预测3D坐标，或依赖复杂图神经网络和等变层。本文旨在提出一种更简洁、直接的自回归生成范式，无需显式键序分配，通过局部坐标编码天然实现SE(3)不变性，并利用强化学习优化生成分子的物理合理性。

Method: ADT采用自回归逐原子生成策略：每个新原子的位置在已放置原子的局部坐标系中编码，从而实现SE(3)不变性；主干为纯因果Transformer，Token序列完整描述3D结构及其化学键图G（无需键序分配）。引入xTB拓扑保持率（XTP）作为评估指标，即生成的分子经xTB GFN2几何弛豫后仍保持原始拓扑G的比例。采用强化学习（RLVR）以xTB奖励函数对预训练模型进行微调。提出逆运动学Transformer处理大分子离散误差问题。

Result: 预训练模型在GEOM-Drugs数据集上XTP约54%，有效分子产率约50%。经RLVR强化学习微调后，XTP提升至约98%，有效分子产率约95%，同时保持GEOM-Drugs数据集的分子大小和组成分布。逆运动学Transformer可恢复大分子因离散误差下降的XTP。

Conclusion: ADT证明了纯因果Transformer通过局部坐标编码即可实现SE(3)等变的3D分子自回归生成，结合可验证xTB奖励的强化学习能显著提升生成分子的物理合理性。该方法为直接3D分子生成提供了简洁有效的新范式。

Abstract: We present an SE(3)-invariant transformer for 3D-molecule generation,
  the Atomic Design Transformer (ADT). ADT places atoms one
  at a time, autoregressively. SE(3) invariance is achieved by
  tokenization: each new atom's position is encoded in the local
  coordinate frame of a previously placed atom. The backbone is a plain
  causal transformer. The token stream fully specifies a 3D structure
  together with its chemical-bond graph G, without any bond-order
  assignment. To score generated molecules we introduce the xTB
  topology-preservation rate (XTP): the fraction of molecules for
  which an xTB GFN2 relaxation preserves G specified by the token stream.
  For XTP-accepted molecules we also report the
  relaxation energy and the root mean square of the atomic displacement (RMSD). We evaluate
  two ADT models. The first is ADT pretrained on the GEOM-Drugs
  $\le\!30$-heavy-atom dataset; we benchmark scaffold-conditioned 3D
  generation across seven drug-like scaffolds from the model. It
  reaches an XTP of ${\sim}54\%$ and a valid-molecule yield
  $N^{\mathrm{gen}}/N$ of ${\sim}50\%$, where $N^{\mathrm{gen}}/N$ is the
  fraction of samples that are distinct, topology-preserving, and
  chemically valid. The second model continues from the first by
  reinforcement learning against the verifiable xTB reward (RLVR), using
  no external molecules. RLVR raises XTP to ${\sim}98\%$ and
  $N^{\mathrm{gen}}/N$ to ${\sim}95\%$, while approximately preserving the
  GEOM-Drugs size and composition distributions. Finally, we present
  an Inverse-Kinematics Transformer that recovers XTP for large molecules, where discretization error accumulates. ADT thus enables direct 3D generation.

</details>


### [87] [CADAQUES: A Cost-Aware Dual Architecture for Query-Efficient Autonomous Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16127)
*Jorge Bravo-Abad*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: CADAQUES是一个将成本作为一等原语的开源Python框架，通过Oracle-Driver双协议分离发现循环，使用向量值预算追踪多种成本（墙钟时间、CPU小时、货币成本、语言模型token），并采用仅追加账本记录交易前后成本。在二维Ising模型临界温度定位任务中验证，低 fidelity 探索+高 fidelity 精炼策略优于全程高 fidelity 方案，计量开销仅数十微秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主发现系统继承数值优化的控制结构，固定迭代次数、忽略查询成本差异、将决策视为免费，而实际中查询成本可能相差数个数量级，基于大语言模型或昂贵代理模型的规划器本身也消耗大量资源。

Method: 将发现循环解耦为Oracle（回答查询）和Driver（提出查询）两个结构协议；引入向量值预算（墙钟时间、CPU小时、货币成本、语言模型token）统一计量评估与决策成本；采用仅追加账本记录每次交易执行前声明的成本和执行后结算的成本，使两者差异成为可观测属性。

Result: 在含噪的二维Ising模型临界温度定位任务中，噪声环境下聚焦最佳观测结果的策略会被噪声诱导的峰值误导，而先使用廉价低 fidelity 查询探索、再以高 fidelity 查询精炼的策略，在给定预算下误差更低且更稳定。计量开销约数十微秒/迭代，比最便宜的 oracle 查询低三个数量级。

Conclusion: 成本作为一等原语的架构设计可行且高效，能够使自主发现系统更真实地反映实际计算资源约束，MIT许可证开源。

Abstract: Autonomous discovery systems couple a resource that answers queries (a simulator, instrument, or analytic model) to an algorithm that selects what to query next. Most software frameworks for this loop inherit the control structure of numerical optimization: campaigns run for a fixed number of iterations, query costs are absent from the programming interface, and decision-making is treated as free. In practice, queries may differ in cost by orders of magnitude, and planners built on large language models or expensive surrogates consume resources of their own. Here we present CADAQUES, an open-source Python framework built on one architectural principle: cost is a first-class primitive of the discovery loop. CADAQUES separates the loop into two structural protocols, an Oracle that answers queries and a Driver that proposes them, and charges both evaluations and decisions against a common vector-valued budget spanning wall time, CPU hours, monetary cost, and language model tokens. An append-only ledger records, for each transaction, the cost declared before execution and the cost settled afterwards, making their discrepancy an observable property of the campaign. We evaluate the architecture by locating the critical temperature of the two-dimensional Ising model from noisy finite-size estimates against the exact thermodynamic-limit reference. In this noisy setting, strategies that concentrate around the best observed result can be misled by noise-induced peaks, whereas a schedule that explores with cheap low-fidelity queries and refines with higher-fidelity ones yields lower and less variable errors than high fidelity throughout, at the studied budget scale. Metering adds tens of microseconds per iteration, three orders of magnitude below the cheapest oracle query. The framework is MIT-licensed and archived at Zenodo (doi:10.5281/zenodo.21293589).

</details>

### [88] [Fragmented ETH: Prethermalization, Timescales, and Ensemble Inequivalence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15350)
*C. L. Sriram,Soumya Kanti Pal,Lea F. Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究具有强长程相互作用的有限量子系统趋近热平衡的过程。由于从全连接极限继承的近似守恒量导致希尔伯特空间碎片化，系统呈现能带分裂的多体谱，从而产生异常缓慢的平衡化和长寿命的预热平台。作者揭示了哪些可观测量和初态会表现出或规避预热平台的机制，并发展了微扰理论来解析计算预热平台的高度和时间尺度。尽管全局遍历性缺失，但单个能带内发展出量子混沌，支持能带分辨的热化描述（fETH）。与传统ETH不同，fETH的有限尺寸标度服从对称性选择定则，限制了可比对的系统尺寸。这种能带分辨描述直接导致微正则系综与正则系综的不等价性，而无需依赖平衡相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有强长程相互作用的有限量子系统如何趋近热平衡，特别是希尔伯特空间碎片化对热化动力学和统计力学的影响，并解释微正则与正则系综不等价的微观起源。

Method: 理论分析结合微扰理论，发展能带分辨的特征态热化假说（fETH），通过对称性选择定则约束有限尺寸标度分析。

Result: 发现两阶段平衡化过程非普适；确定预热平台出现/规避的条件；给出平台高度和时间尺度的解析表达式；建立fETH框架并揭示系综不等价机制。

Conclusion: 希尔伯特空间碎片化导致的热化行为不同于标准ETH，fETH为理解碎片化系统中的热化提供了新框架，系综不等价源自能带分辨描述的微正则与正则系综的结构差异。

Abstract: We investigate how finite quantum systems with strong long-range interactions approach thermal equilibrium. Nearly conserved quantities inherited from the fully connected limit fragment the Hilbert space and give rise to a many-body spectrum split into energy bands. As a result, equilibration becomes anomalously slow and proceeds through long-lived prethermal plateaus. This two-stage equilibration process is, however, not universal. We uncover the mechanism that determines which observables and initial states exhibit, or evade, prethermal plateaus. We also develop a perturbative theory that provides analytical expressions for both the height of the prethermal plateau and its timescale. Despite the lack of global ergodicity, quantum chaos develops within individual energy bands, enabling the definition of microcanonical ensembles within the bands. This supports a band-resolved formulation of thermalization, which we term fragmented eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (fETH). Unlike conventional ETH, finite-size scaling in fETH obeys a symmetry-imposed selection rule that restricts which system sizes can be compared. This band-resolved description has direct consequences for equilibrium statistical mechanics. While microcanonical ensembles remain confined to a single band, canonical ensembles mix different bands. This mismatch explains ensemble inequivalence without invoking equilibrium phase transitions. Our results apply to a broad class of Hamiltonians exhibiting Hilbert-space fragmentation.

</details>


### [89] [Scaling regimes of the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation from the functional renormalization group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15784)
*Liubov Gosteva,Nicolás Wschebor,Léonie Canet*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了随机Kuramoto-Sivashinsky (KS) 方程的重整化群(RG)方法，指出以往基于锐截止的微扰Wilson RG方法虽然得到定性正确的结果，但在取动量导数时存在内在发散问题。作者采用光滑截断的功能重整化群(FRG)框架建立了KS模型的流方程，证明了在大尺度下流向了Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ)不动点。进一步计算了宽动量-频率范围内的两点关联函数，揭示了三个普适标度区域：KPZ区(z=3/2)、Edwards-Wilkinson区(z=2)和最近发现的无粘区(z=1)，后者源于有效粘度的消失。最后研究了确定论KS方程在大尺度下的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期基于锐截断的Wilson RG在处理KS方程时，取动量导数在某些情况下不是良好定义的，导致固有发散。虽然这些方法得到了定性正确的结果，但方法论上存在问题，需要更严谨的框架来修正。

Method: 采用光滑截断的功能重整化群(FRG)框架，建立了KS模型的流方程，计算了宽动量-频率范围内的两点关联函数，并分析了确定论KS方程在大尺度下的行为。

Result: (1) KS模型在FRG下流向KPZ不动点；(2) 两点关联函数存在三个普适标度区域：KPZ区(z=3/2)、EW区(z=2)和无粘区(z=1)；(3) 确定论KS方程在噪声趋于零时，大尺度上仍可表现出KPZ标度行为。

Conclusion: 光滑截断的FRG框架可以有效解决锐截断Wilson RG在处理KS方程时的内在发散问题，提供了更严格的RG分析，并揭示了更丰富的普适标度行为。

Abstract: We revisit the renormalization group (RG) approach to the one-dimensional stochastic Kuramoto-Sivashinsky (KS) equation and show that previous approaches based on perturbative Wilsonian RG with a sharp cutoff are not valid, even though they yield a qualitatively correct picture. The reason is that taking momentum derivatives while using the sharp cutoff is not well-defined in some cases and leads to intrinsic divergencies. This is a well-known problem of Wilsonian RG, which can be simply cured by using a smooth cutoff, and employing the functional renormalization group (FRG) framework. We establish the flow equations for the KS model within the FRG, and demonstrate that it flows to the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) fixed point at large scales. We then calculate the full two-point correlation function over a wide range of momenta and frequencies. We show that it exhibits three universal scaling regimes that we characterize: the KPZ regime (with dynamical exponent $z=3/2$), the Edwards-Wilkinson regime (with $z=2$) and the recently discovered inviscid regime (with $z=1$). The latter develops over an extended range of large wavenumbers and originates from the vanishing of the effective viscosity. Lastly, we investigate the large-scale behavior of the deterministic KS equation by studying the limit of vanishing noise and we determine the scales where the KPZ regime can emerge in the deterministic case.

</details>


### [90] [Ultrametric organization of energy landscapes on random Erdős--Rényi graphs: topological origin of barrier hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15902)
*A. P. Zubarev*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了稀疏随机Erdős–Rényi图上能量景观的超度量组织。通过构造动力学马氏距离度量，发现超度量度随能量展宽ΔF单调增加（42%→96%），并证明当ΔF→∞时该度量收敛于经典单链超度量。结果表明在大能量展宽极限下，超度量性是稀疏局部树状网络的普适性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究稀疏随机图上能量景观的超度量组织特性，理解在复杂能量景观中动力学过程的几何结构，特别是能量展宽对超度量性质的影响。

Method: 在Erdős–Rényi图上为每个顶点分配随机自由能（均匀分布，宽度ΔF），用Kramers跃迁速率的马尔可夫过程建模动力学，通过速率矩阵谱分解构造吸引盆之间的动力学马氏距离度量，并进行V=5000顶点、E=5000边的计算实验。

Result: 超度量度从ΔF=10 kJ/mol时的≈42%单调增加到ΔF=1000 kJ/mol时的≈96%；证明当ΔF→∞时该度量的对数渐近行为逐点收敛到单链超度量；有限ΔF下次优路径的修正随ΔF增大呈指数抑制。

Conclusion: 在大能量展宽极限下，超度量性是稀疏局部树状网络能量景观的普适性质。

Abstract: We investigate the ultrametric organization of energy landscapes defined on sparse random Erdős--Rényi graphs. Each graph vertex is assigned a random free energy from a uniform distribution over an interval of width $ΔF$, and the kinetics are modeled by a Markov process with Kramers transition rates. Using spectral decomposition of the rate matrix, we construct a kinetic Mahalanobis metric between basins of attraction. Computational experiments for graphs with $V=5000$ vertices and $E=5000$ edges show that the degree of nontrivial ultrametricity increases monotonically from $\approx42\%$ for $ΔF=10$ kJ/mol to $\approx96\%$ for $ΔF=1000$ kJ/mol. We prove a limit theorem: as $ΔF\to\infty$, the logarithmic asymptotics of this metric converge pointwise to the classical single-linkage ultrametric. For finite $ΔF$, corrections from suboptimal paths are exponentially suppressed with increasing $ΔF$, so that the metric becomes asymptotically ultrametric. Our results suggest that ultrametricity is a universal property of sparse, locally tree-like networks with rugged energy landscapes in the limit of large energy spreads.

### [91] [Zigzag ordering, defects, and anomalous relaxation in antiferromagnetic Kuramoto lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15911)
*Priyanka D. Bhoyar,Prashant M. Gade*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了带负最近邻耦合的Kuramoto振子非平衡有序动力学，发现一维系统中缺陷密度呈异常缓慢的粗化行为（~t^{-1/4}），局域持续概率呈拉伸指数衰减（指数α=1/4），临界指数z=2，构成独特的普适类；二维系统中几何阻挫导致长寿命亚稳态畴壁结构。这些结果表明，确定性非线性动力学和几何阻挫本身即可产生慢弛豫和异常标度行为，无需淬火无序或随机噪声。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究确定性非线性动力学与几何阻挫（负最近邻耦合诱导的反铁磁锯齿序）能否在没有淬火无序或随机噪声的条件下，独立产生慢弛豫和异常标度行为，以及这些行为是否构成新的普适类。

Method: 采用耦合Kuramoto振子模型（含负最近邻耦合），通过数值模拟分析一维和二维系统中缺陷密度衰减、局域持续概率和标度指数；利用连续近似和粗粒化偏微分方程进行理论解释，结合线性稳定性分析解释锯齿有序态的出现。

Result: 一维：缺陷密度~t^{-1/4}，饱和时间t_c~N^2（z=2），局域持续概率指数α=1/4，且这些指数与耦合强度无关；二维：几何阻挫阻止完全有序，产生长寿命亚稳态畴壁结构，初始缺陷衰减后出现交叉与饱和。

Conclusion: 确定性非线性动力学和几何阻挫足以独立产生异常缓慢的粗化动力学和标度行为，构成独特的普适类；连续近似和线性稳定性分析成功解释了观测到的异常指数和锯齿有序态的形成机制。

Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium ordering dynamics of coupled Kuramoto oscillators with negative nearest-neighbor coupling, which induces a zigzag antiferromagnetic ordering. In one dimension, the defect density exhibits anomalously slow coarsening, decaying as $(D(t)\sim t^{-1/4})$ before saturating at a system-size-dependent time $(t_c(N)\sim N^z)$ with (z=2). The local persistence probability follows a stretched-exponential form, $(P(t)\sim \exp(-c t^α))$, with $(α=1/4)$. These exponents are observed are independent of the magnitude of the coupling, which merely rescales the characteristic time scale. The equality $(α=δ=1/4)$ together with (z=2) is consistent with a distinct universality class. These results demonstrate that deterministic nonlinear dynamics and geometric frustration alone are sufficient to generate slow relaxation and anomalous scaling, without quenched disorder or stochastic noise. A continuum approximation and the corresponding coarse-grained partial differential equation provide a theoretical explanation for the observed anomalous exponents, while linear stability analysis accounts for the emergence of the zigzag ordered state. In two dimensions, geometric frustration inhibits complete ordering and gives rise to long-lived metastable domain-wall structures. An initial transient defect decay is observed before crossover and saturation. These results demonstrate how frustration and continuous phase variables can fundamentally modify coarsening dynamics and generate anomalously slow relaxation in deterministic many-body systems.

### [92] [Nonequilibrium thermodynamics of feedback-control: a phase-space perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16186)
*José A. Almanza-Marrero*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了包含奇异情况在内的通用反馈控制系统的涨落关系，提出了不可用信息的概念，并通过有限分辨率Szilard引擎证明：当测量信息发散时，同样发散的不可用信息导致可提取功保持有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准麦克斯韦妖问题假设恶魔可获取系统完整相空间信息，但在实际应用中这一假设不成立，因此需要研究更通用的反馈控制系统。

Method: 推导通用反馈控制系统的涨落关系，引入广义不可用信息概念，并通过有限分辨率Szilard引擎进行理论验证。

Result: 在高分辨率极限下，恶魔获取的信息量可能发散，但可提取功保持有限；这是因为同时有等量发散的信息变为不可用信息。

Conclusion: 揭示了信息获取与功提取之间的根本限制：获取的信息并非全部可用于做功，不可用信息的存在解释了信息发散而功有限的悖论。

Abstract: Maxwell demons can convert knowledge into thermodynamic advantage by using measurement-acquired information. However, standard formulations of this problem assume that the demon has access to the system's entire phase space, an assumption that fails in many practical applications. Here, I address this problem by deriving fluctuation relations for general feedback-controlled systems, including such singular cases. The central quantity is a generalized notion of unavailable information: a portion of the acquired information that cannot be used to extract useful work. Finally, a Szilard engine with finite resolution illustrates these results. In the high-resolution limit, the information acquired by the demon may diverge, yet the extractable work remains finite. This work shows that this occurs because an equally divergent amount of information becomes unavailable.

</details>
